After a couple of listens, I'm starting to realize this guy might be a genius. Or at least smarter than we all think. This whole production was incredibly well put together. Not only that, but his acting skills are really good. His tone of voice, the small mannerisms, facial expressions, and confidence on camera makes it feel like he was very intentional with how he wanted to portray himself. I found the irony behind the contrast of his suburban character and hard hitting type music to be hilarious. It was funny without being corny, and that's because his musical ability is impressive and enjoyable to listen to. It's the perfect recipe for a viral sensation. And the effort he put forth, I think, is underappreciated.
